 ) supreme court ne mahilaon ke adhikaar se judi ek badi tippanee kii he
 The court has said during the hearing of a case that the husband cannot ask his wife to co-exist
 darasal, ek mahila kii taraf se pati par krurta kaa aarope lagaaya gaya tha
 The Supreme Court made this remark during the hearing of the case related to it
 mahila ne apane aarope main kaha tha ki pati chahta he ki vah uske saath rahe lekin vah apane pati ke saath nahin rahanaa chaahati he
 Keeping in mind this pain of the woman, the Supreme Court made strict remarks against the husband
 court ne kaha ki patni koi 'chal sampati' yaa 'vastu' nahin he
 Therefore, despite the desire to be with the wife, the husband cannot press the wife for this
 court ne kya kahajustise madan bi lokur or deepak gupta kii peeth ne adaalat main maujuud mahila ke pati se kaha, 'vah ek chal sampatti nahin he
 You can't force it
 vah aapke saath nahin rahanaa chaahati hai
 How can you tell that you will be with him

 The Ministry of Human Resource Development is considering setting up an External Peer Review (EPR) mechanism for central universities on the lines of the rules to be followed in Indian Institutes of Technology (iits)
 sutron ne bataaya ki ek haalia baithak main maanav sansaadhan vikaas mantri smriti irani ne apane adhikariyon se kaha ki ve iaiti kii tarj par kendriya vishvavidhyalayon ke akalan ke liye bhi bahari pear samiksha (eepiaar) tantra shuru karne kii sambhaavna par vichaar karen
 "an external peer review is a mechanism under which a committee of experts from teaching, research and industry assess the performance of an IIT on certain set standards every five years," an official source said
 mantri ke suzav ke baad mantralay is vyavastha ko kendriya vishvavidhyalayon ke liye bhi shuru karne kii sambhaavna par vichaar kar rahaa he 
 '' Comments desh main 40 se zyada kendriya vishvavidhyalay hai or sambhav he ki kisi ek vishvavidhyalay ke adhikariyon kii team tay kiye gaye swaroop ke aadhaar par anya kii samiksha kare
 However, necessary steps will be taken to finalize the nature of such a review
 sutron ne bataaya ki vishvavidhyalay anudaan ayog (ujisi) ko bhi vishvavidhyalayon ke liye pear samiksha prakriya ke byore ko antim rup dene ke kaam main shaamil kiya ja saktaa he 
 In a recent meeting, sources said, HRD Minister Smriti Irani asked her officials to consider the possibility of introducing an external peer review (EPR) mechanism to assess central universities on the lines of iits
 ek aadhikarik sutara ne bataaya, ‘‘bahari pear samiksha ek aisa tantra he jiske tahat shikshan, shodh evam udyog ke visheshgyon kii ek samiti har paanch saal par kuch tay maanakon par kisi iaiti ke pradarshan kaa akalan karte hai
 Following the minister's suggestion, the ministry is considering the possibility of introducing this system for central universities as well
 ’’ tippaniyan There are more than 40 central universities in the country and it is possible that teams of officials of one university review the other based on the format decided
 baharhaal, aisi samiksha ke swaroop ko antim rup dene ke liye jaruri kadam uthaae jaaenge

 golibari ke baad police ne pej ko maar giraaya tha
 Even after several days of investigation into the firing incident at the gurdwara, federal agencies say that they have not received any information about the reasons behind it
 agenciyon ko abhi tak is bare main koi jaankaree nahin he ki kis vajah se purv sainik ne golibari kii is bhayankar ghatana ko anjaam diya
 He fears that the reason behind the incident also ended with the attacker's death
 milwauki gurudware main golibari kii ghatana ke baad police ne 41 varshiya purv sainik vade maaikel ko maar giraaya tha
 The agencies say that now perhaps the reason behind the incident will never be known
 ‘sienen’ ke mutabik ok creek ke police pramukh jon edwards kaa kahana he, ‘‘ant main shaayad hamaare paas is bare main bahut saare tathy hon ki vah kin chizon se judaa hua tha, vah kiske saath judaa hua tha, lekin shaayad ham uski manshaa ke bare main kabhi jaan nahin sakenge, kyonki vah mar gaya he, or manshaa bhi uske saath hi mar gai he
 '' jaanchakarta vibhinn rajyon main isse jude taron ko khangaal rahe hai lekin media main aayi khabaron ke anusaar kanoon visheshgyon kaa maananaa he ki unhen in tathyon ko adaalat main pesh karne kaa mauka nahin milegaa
 Right now, information about the attacker's house, family, friends, personal data, his old criminal records etc
 is being made
 ullekhneey he ki epabiai is puure maamle kii jaanch kii rahi he lekin usne bahut kam jaankaree saarvajanik kii he
 The agency is also investigating the aspect of racial hatred during its investigation
 yahaan khaas baat yah he ki america ke visconcin sthit gurudware main golibari karne vaala vade maaikel pej yahaan ke sangheey jaanch beuro (epabiai) ke radar par bilkul nahin tha
 However, some private groups were secretly keeping an eye on him
 ab yah spasht ho chukaa he ki kam se kam do nijee samooh ‘anti-diphameshan lig’ or ‘south pavarty lau centre’ beete kuch saal se pej kii gatividhiyon par najar banaae hue the
 These groups keep an eye on extremist and hate-mongering individuals-organizations
 duusari ore, epabiai ko is shaks ke khatarnaak mansoobon ke bare main koi jaankaree nahin thi
 He says Page was not on his radar
 epabiai ke pravaktaa paul bresan ne kaha, ‘‘aapraadhik gatividhiyon kii jaanch karne ke saath america nagarikon kii swatantraaa kaa santulan bananaa hamaare liye rojaanaa ek chunauti hoti he
 How aggressive an idea is expressed, but it is not a crime for us
 ’’ Meanwhile, 'anti-defamation League' convenor Marilyn Mayo said, "when we know that someone is talking about extremist violent action, we share this information with the Justice Department here
" parantu is shaks ke bare main hamane sochaa nahin tha ki vah is tarah kaa kadam uthaane ja rahaa he
 "india's Ambassador to the US Nirupama Rao met the families of the victims of the firing at the Oak Creek Gurdwara in Wisconsin, and assured full help

 tippaniyan The officials told the Indian ambassador how the incident happened and what steps are being taken to protect the people of the Sikh community
 nirupama mangalvaar kii shaam nikaale gaye candal march main bhi shamil huin

 vah gurudwara ke adhyaksh divangat satvant singh kaleka sahit sabhi peediton ke rishtedaaron se milin
 Kaleka attempted to stop the attacker and died, saving the lives of the people
 golibari kii ghatana main hamalavar sahit saat log maare gaye the

 uske shweton kii shreshthata maanane vaale nasli unmaadiyon kaa sanghathan se jude hone kii suchanaaen hai

" ’’ According to ABC News, a federal law official says that Cook was prohibited from possessing weapons after he was previously convicted in a case
 isi kaaran use hathiyaar rakhane ke aarope main giraftaar kiya gaya he
 In 2002, Cook was accused of fleeing by tricking a traffic policeman
 ravivaar ko gurudware main golicond karne vaale 41 varshiya pej ke saath cook kaa sambandh is ghatana ke kuch saptaah pehle hi tutaa tha
 Six people were killed in this attack
 police ne cook ke ghar kii jaanch ke dauraan vahaan se ek bandook baraamad kii he lekin unka kahana he ki iskaa upyog golibari cond main nahin hua he
 Cook has lived in two separate apartments in South Miliwaki with Page
 sangheey agenciyon ko abhi tak is bare main koi jaankaree nahin he ki aakhir purv sainik pej ne yah golibari kyon kii or iske pichhi uski manshaa kya thi
 Page was killed by police after the shootout
 gurudware main hui golibari kii ghatana kii jaanch ke kai din baad bhi sangheey agenciyon kaa kahana he ki unhen iske peeche ke kaarnon ke bare main koi jaankaree nahin mil paayi he
 The agencies do not yet have any information about the reason why the ex-servicemen carried out this horrific firing incident
 unhen dar he ki ghatana ke peeche kaa kaaran bhi hamalavar kii maut ke saath hi samaapt ho gaya
 Police killed 41-year-old ex-soldier Wade Michael after the shooting incident at the Milwaukee Gurdwara
 agenciyon kaa kahana he ki ab shaayad ghatana ke peeche kii vajah ke bare main kabhi pataa nahi chal paaegaa
 According to CNN, Oak Creek Police Chief John Edwards says, "in the end we probably have a lot of facts about what he was involved with, who he was connected to, but maybe we You will never know about the intention, because he has died, and the intention is also dead with him
 ’’ Investigators are tracing the wires connected to it in various states, but according to media reports, law experts believe that they will not get a chance to present these facts in court
 philhal, hamalavar ke ghar, parivaar, doston, vyaktigat aankade, uske puraane aapraadhik record aadi ke bare main pataa kiya ja rahaa he
 It is noteworthy that the FBI is investigating this entire case but has made very little information public
 agency apni is jaanch ke dauraan nasli ghrinaa ke pahalu ke bare main bhi tahakikat kar rahi he

 alabatta us par kuch nijee samooh gupt rup se najar banaae hue the

 ye samooh ativaadee or nafrat failaane vaale vyaktiyon-sanghathanon par najar rakhte hai

 uskaa kahana he ki pej uske radar par nahin tha

 '' udhar, ‘anti-diphameshan lig’ kii sanyojak marlin myo ne kaha, ‘‘jab ham jaanate hai ki koi ativaadee hinsak karrwai ke bare main baat kar rahaa he to ham isaki jaankaree yahaan ke nyaay vibhaag ke saath saajha karte hai
 But we did not think about this person that he is going to take such a step
 ’’ america main bharat kii rajdoot nirupama raav ne visconcin ke ok creek gurudware main hui golibari ke peedit pariwaron se mulaakaat kar puri madad kaa bharosa diya

 unhen epabiai or sthaneey police ke adhikariyon ne ghatana kii jaanch ke bare main jaankaree di

 candal march is ghatana main maare gaye logon ke sammaan main nikaala gaya tha

 kaleka ne hamalavar ko rokane kaa prayaas kiya tha or logon kii jaan bachaate hue unki maut ho gai thi
